 * Government is not allowed to take multi-cropped irrigated land for private companies or for public purposes for private purposes
 achchhah sarkaar ne spasht kiya he ki ek samay seemaa ke bheetar saarvajanik uddeshy kya hota he

 is tarah kii jameen kii keemat zyada tay karnaa behatar vikalp hota
 Farmers' Consent * The bill states that if the government acquires land for the purpose of private companies for public purposes, then at least 80% of the affected families need to be approved for the proposed acquisition
 * lekin agar sarkaar apane paas rakhane, niyantrit karne yaa istemaal ke liye jameen leti he to kisi rajamandi kii jarurat nahin hogi
 The use of 'emergency clause', under which land can be taken without consent, is limited to rare cases such as national security and natural disasters
 achchhah 'argency cloj', jiskaa noida main vyapak rup se istemaal kiya gaya, ke istemaal ko simit karnaa swaagatyogy he
 Bad: The government can acquire land for itself without taking the opinion of majority farmers
 muaavja* sarkaar kii ore se adhigrahit bhoomi kaa muaavja gramin ilaakon main jameen kii bazaar dar se chah guna se kam nahin hona chahie or shahari ilaakon main jameen kii bazaar dar se doguna se kam nahin hona chahie
